GT Equivalence Verification (CRK16)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_f*A**c2
Candidate formulas: 78

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
0.9709294495916855\,A^{1/3}-0.24581249010242617\,A.
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) have no residual \(t\)-dependence after choosing parameters, and (ii) reduce exactly to a linear combination of \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A\) with those coefficients (for all \(A\) in the domain).

---

### 1. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + A c2\sin(c3 t+c4)\)
Set \(c2=0\) to remove the sine term. Then choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855,\; c1=-0.24581249010242617\). Matches GT.

### 2. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(c3 t+c4)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then pick \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 3. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(c3\exp(Ac4+c5 t)+c6)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then pick \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 4. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3}\sin(c4 t+c5)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then pick \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 5. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then pick \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 6. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1\cos(c2|A|) + Ac3\)
To match GT for all \(A\), the extra \(A^{1/3}\cos(\cdot)\) term must vanish or become a constant multiple of \(A^{1/3}\). Easiest: set \(c1=0\). Then choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855,\; c3=-0.24581249010242617\). Matches.

### 7. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2 e^{Ac3}\)
Need the exponential term gone: set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 8. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3\)
Make the extra power term vanish: set \(c3=0\). Then choose \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 9. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2|A|^{c3}\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 10. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2|A|/(c3+|A|)\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0, c1\) as above. Matches.

### 11. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1\)
Directly choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855,\; c1=-0.24581249010242617\). Matches.

### 12. \(c0|A|^{1/3} + c1|A|\)
This uses \(|A|\) and \(|A|^{1/3}\), not \(A\) and \(A^{1/3}\). It cannot equal GT for all real \(A\) (sign mismatch for negative \(A\)); only could match on a restricted domain \(A\ge 0\), but equivalence here is for all feature values. No match.

### 13. \(c0|A|^{1/3} + c1|A| + c2|A|^{1/3}\)
Same issue as 12 (absolute values). No match for all real \(A\).

### 14. \(Ac0 + c1|A|^{1/3}\)
Absolute value in the \(1/3\) power prevents matching for negative \(A\). No match.

### 15. \(Ac0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3\)
To match GT, need an \(A^{1/3}\) term and no constant term. Set \(c3=0\), set \(c1=1/3\), set \(c2=0.9709294495916855\), and set \(c0=-0.24581249010242617\). Matches.

### 16. \(c0|A|^{1/3} + c1 + c2|A|\)
Absolute values + constant term. Even setting \(c1=0\), still \(|A|\) vs \(A\). No match.

### 17. \(Ac0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\)
Absolute value and constant. No match.

### 18. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2\)
Set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0, c1\) as GT. Matches.

### 19. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + c3\)
Need no constant: set \(c3=0\). Combine \(A\)-terms: choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855\) and \(c1+c2=-0.24581249010242617\) (many solutions, e.g. \(c1=-0.2458,\;c2=0\)). Matches.

### 20. \(c0|A|^{1/3} + c1\sin(c2|A|+c3)\)
Absolute value and sine; to remove sine set \(c1=0\), leaving \(c0|A|^{1/3}\) which cannot produce the \(-0.2458A\) term and also has \(|A|^{1/3}\). No match.

### 21. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2|A|^2\)

### 22. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2\log(Ac3+1)\)
